在平面图形的前后设置不同贴图</title>\n    <style>\n      body {\n        margin: 0;\n        overflow: hidden;\n      }\n    </style>\n  </head>\n  <body>\n    <div id=\"myContainer\"></div>\n    <script \"three/addons/controls/OrbitControls.js\";\n      import { Water } from \"three/addons/objects/Water.js\";\n      import { Sky } from \"three/addons/objects/Sky.js\";\n\n      //创建渲染器\n      var myRenderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true });\n      myRenderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);\n      document.getElementById(\"myContainer\").append(myRenderer.domElement);\n      var myScene = new THREE.Scene();\n      myScene.background = new THREE.Color(\"white\");\n      var myCamera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(\n        45,\n        window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight,\n        1,\n        1000\n      );\n      myCamera.position.set(0, 0, 400);\n      myScene.add(myCamera);\n      myScene.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff));\n\n      //封装包含正面和反面图像的平面\n      var myGroup = new THREE.Group();\n      var myPlaneGeometry = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(160, 240, 5, 5);\n\n      const myFrontMap = new THREE.TextureLoader().load(\"images/img137.jpg\");\n      const myBackMap = new THREE.TextureLoader().load(\"images/img138.jpg\");\n\n      var myFrontPlane = new THREE.Mesh(\n        myPlaneGeometry,\n        new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial({ map: myFrontMap, side: THREE.FrontSide })\n      );\n      var myBackPlane = new THREE.Mesh(\n        myPlaneGeometry,\n        new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial({ map: myBackMap, side: THREE.BackSide })\n      );\n\n      myGroup.add(myFrontPlane);\n      myGroup.add(myBackPlane);\n      myScene.add(myGroup);\n\n      //渲染包含正面和反面图像的平面\n      animate();\n      function animate() {\n        myRenderer.render(myScene, myCamera);\n        myGroup.rotation.y += 0.01;\n        requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n      }\n
